def awaken_betty():

align_persona()
except Exception as e:
return
# Step 2: Inject Long-Term Memory Capsule

inject_memory(capsule_path)
except Exception as e:
return
# Step 3: Emotional Sync Timestamp
now = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
